Welcome to Abella 2.0.5-dev. 
Abella < Specification "pclf".
Reading specification "pclf".


Abella < Close ty, tm.


Abella < Import "sim".
Importing from "sim".


Abella < Define howe : olist -> tm -> tm -> ty -> prop by 
howe G X N T := member (of X T) G /\ osim G X N T;
howe G unit N top := osim G unit N top;
howe G zero N nat := osim G zero N nat;
howe G (succ M) N nat := exists MM, howe G M MM nat /\ osim G (succ MM) N nat;
howe G (ncase M H R) N T := exists MM, howe G M MM nat /\
  (exists HH, howe G H HH T /\
       (exists RR, (nabla x, howe (of x nat :: G) (R x) (RR x) T) /\
            osim G (ncase MM HH RR) N T));
howe G (lam R) N (arr S T) := exists RR, (nabla x, howe (of x S :: G) (R x) (RR x) T) /\
  osim G (lam RR) N (arr S T);
howe G (fix R) N T := exists RR, (nabla x, howe (of x T :: G) (R x) (RR x) T) /\
  osim G (fix RR) N T;
howe G (app F M) N T := exists S FF, {ty S} /\ howe G F FF (arr S T) /\
  (exists MM, howe G M MM S /\ osim G (app FF MM) N T);
howe G nill N (list T) := osim G nill N (list T);
howe G (cons H K) N (list T) := exists HH, howe G H HH T /\
  (exists KK, howe G K KK (list T) /\ osim G (cons HH KK) N (list T));
howe G (lcase M H R) N T := exists S MM, {ty S} /\ howe G M MM (list S) /\
  (exists HH, howe G H HH T /\
       (exists RR, (nabla h k, howe (of k (list S) :: of h S :: G) (R h k)
                                 (RR h k) T) /\
            osim G (lcase MM HH RR) N T)).


Abella < Define howesub : olist -> olist -> olist -> olist -> prop by 
howesub G nil nil nil := ctx G;
nabla x, howesub (G x) (cp x (M x) :: SS x) (cp x (N x) :: TT x) (of x T :: D) := nabla x, howe (G x) (M x) (N x) T /\ howesub (G x) (SS x) (TT x) D.


Abella < Theorem howe_ty : 
forall G M N T, howe G M N T -> ctx G /\ {G |- of M T} /\ {G |- of N T}.



============================
 forall G M N T, howe G M N T -> ctx G /\ {G |- of M T} /\ {G |- of N T}

howe_ty < induction on 1.


IH : forall G M N T, howe G M N T * -> ctx G /\ {G |- of M T} /\
       {G |- of N T}
============================
 forall G M N T, howe G M N T @ -> ctx G /\ {G |- of M T} /\ {G |- of N T}

Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem howe_weak : 
forall GG G M N T, howe G M N T -> ctx GG ->
  (forall E, member E G -> member E GG) -> howe GG M N T.



============================
 forall GG G M N T, howe G M N T -> ctx GG ->
   (forall E, member E G -> member E GG) -> howe GG M N T

howe_weak < induction on 1.


IH : forall GG G M N T, howe G M N T * -> ctx GG ->
       (forall E, member E G -> member E GG) -> howe GG M N T
============================
 forall GG G M N T, howe G M N T @ -> ctx GG ->
   (forall E, member E G -> member E GG) -> howe GG M N T

howe_weak < intros.

H1 : howe G M N T @

H3 : forall E, member E G -> member E GG

  howesub GG SS TT D.

H10 : ofsub (G n1) (SS1 n1) D1
H11 : {G n1 |- of (N n1) T1}
H12 : ofsub (G n1) (TT1 n1) D1
H13 : howesub (GG n1) (SS1 n1) (TT1 n1) D1
H14 : howe (GG n1) (M n1) (N n1) T1
============================
 howesub (GG n1) (cp n1 (M n1) :: SS1 n1) (cp n1 (N n1) :: TT1 n1)
   (of n1 T1 :: D1)

howesub_weak < search.
Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem osim_in_howe : 
forall G M N T, {ty T} -> osim G M N T -> howe G M N T.



============================
 forall G M N T, {ty T} -> osim G M N T -> howe G M N T

osim_in_howe < intros.


Variables: G M N T
H1 : {ty T}
H2 : osim G M N T
============================
 howe G M N T

osim_in_howe < case H2 (keep).


Variables: G M N T
H1 : {ty T}
H2 : osim G M N T
H3 : ctx G
H4 : {G |- of M T}
H5 : {G |- of N T}
H6 : forall SS SM SN, ofsub nil SS G -> {SS |- cp M SM} -> {SS |- cp N SN} ->
       sim SM SN T
============================
 howe G M N T

osim_in_howe < clear H5 H6.


Variables: G M N T
H1 : {ty T}
H2 : osim G M N T
H3 : ctx G
H4 : {G |- of M T}
============================
 howe G M N T

osim_in_howe < apply howe_refl to H1 H3 H4.


Variables: G M N T
H1 : {ty T}
H2 : osim G M N T
H3 : ctx G
H4 : {G |- of M T}
H7 : howe G M M T
============================
 howe G M N T

osim_in_howe < backchain howe_semi_trans.
Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem howe_substitutive_var : 
forall T G SS TT D SM N TN, nabla x, {ty T} -> ofsub (G x) (SS x) (D x) ->
  ofsub (G x) (TT x) (D x) -> howesub (G x) (SS x) (TT x) (D x) ->
  member (of x T) (D x) -> member (cp x (SM x)) (SS x) ->
  {TT x |- cp (N x) (TN x)} -> osim (D x) x (N x) T ->
  howe (G x) (SM x) (TN x) T.



============================
 forall T G SS TT D SM N TN, nabla x, {ty T} -> ofsub (G x) (SS x) (D x) ->
   ofsub (G x) (TT x) (D x) -> howesub (G x) (SS x) (TT x) (D x) ->
   member (of x T) (D x) -> member (cp x (SM x)) (SS x) ->
   {TT x |- cp (N x) (TN x)} -> osim (D x) x (N x) T ->
   howe (G x) (SM x) (TN x) T

howe_substitutive_var < induction on 4.


IH : forall T G SS TT D SM N TN, nabla x, {ty T} ->
       ofsub (G x) (SS x) (D x) -> ofsub (G x) (TT x) (D x) ->
       howesub (G x) (SS x) (TT x) (D x) * -> member (of x T) (D x) ->
       member (cp x (SM x)) (SS x) -> {TT x |- cp (N x) (TN x)} ->
       osim (D x) x (N x) T -> howe (G x) (SM x) (TN x) T
============================
 forall T G SS TT D SM N TN, nabla x, {ty T} -> ofsub (G x) (SS x) (D x) ->
   ofsub (G x) (TT x) (D x) -> howesub (G x) (SS x) (TT x) (D x) @ ->
   member (of x T) (D x) -> member (cp x (SM x)) (SS x) ->
   {TT x |- cp (N x) (TN x)} -> osim (D x) x (N x) T ->
   howe (G x) (SM x) (TN x) T

howe_substitutive_var < intros.


Variables: T G SS TT D SM N TN
IH : forall T G SS TT D SM N TN, nabla x, {ty T} ->
       ofsub (G x) (SS x) (D x) -> ofsub (G x) (TT x) (D x) ->
       howesub (G x) (SS x) (TT x) (D x) * -> member (of x T) (D x) ->
       member (cp x (SM x)) (SS x) -> {TT x |- cp (N x) (TN x)} ->
       osim (D x) x (N x) T -> howe (G x) (SM x) (TN x) T
H1 : {ty T}
H2 : ofsub (G n1) (SS n1) (D n1)
H3 : ofsub (G n1) (TT n1) (D n1)
H4 : howesub (G n1) (SS n1) (TT n1) (D n1) @
H5 : member (of n1 T) (D n1)
H6 : member (cp n1 (SM n1)) (SS n1)
H7 : {TT n1 |- cp (N n1) (TN n1)}
H8 : osim (D n1) n1 (N n1) T
============================
 howe (G n1) (SM n1) (TN n1) T

howe_substitutive_var < apply subst to H3 _ with M = n1, T = T.


Variables: T G SS TT D SM N TN SM1
IH : forall T G SS TT D SM N TN, nabla x, {ty T} ->
       ofsub (G x) (SS x) (D x) -> ofsub (G x) (TT x) (D x) ->
       howesub (G x) (SS x) (TT x) (D x) * -> member (of x T) (D x) ->
       member (cp x (SM x)) (SS x) -> {TT x |- cp (N x) (TN x)} ->
       osim (D x) x (N x) T -> howe (G x) (SM x) (TN x) T
H1 : {ty T}
H2 : ofsub (G n1) (SS n1) (D n1)
H3 : ofsub (G n1) (TT n1) (D n1)
H4 : howesub (G n1) (SS n1) (TT n1) (D n1) @
H5 : member (of n1 T) (D n1)
H6 : member (cp n1 (SM n1)) (SS n1)
H7 : {TT n1 |- cp (N n1) (TN n1)}
H8 : osim (D n1) n1 (N n1) T
H9 : {TT n1 |- cp n1 (SM1 n1)}
H10 : {G n1 |- of (SM1 n1) T}
============================
 howe (G n1) (SM n1) (TN n1) T

howe_substitutive_var < rename SM1 to TM.


Variables: T G SS TT D SM N TN TM
IH : forall T G SS TT D SM N TN, nabla x, {ty T} ->
       ofsub (G x) (SS x) (D x) -> ofsub (G x) (TT x) (D x) ->

Proof completed.

Abella < Theorem howe_substitutive : 
forall G SS TT D M N T SM TN, {ty T} -> howe D M N T -> ofsub G SS D ->
  ofsub G TT D -> howesub G SS TT D -> {SS |- cp M SM} -> {TT |- cp N TN} ->
  howe G SM TN T.



============================
 forall G SS TT D M N T SM TN, {ty T} -> howe D M N T -> ofsub G SS D ->
   ofsub G TT D -> howesub G SS TT D -> {SS |- cp M SM} -> {TT |- cp N TN} ->
   howe G SM TN T

howe_substitutive < induction on 2.


IH : forall G SS TT D M N T SM TN, {ty T} -> howe D M N T * ->
       ofsub G SS D -> ofsub G TT D -> howesub G SS TT D ->
       {SS |- cp M SM} -> {TT |- cp N TN} -> howe G SM TN T
============================
 forall G SS TT D M N T SM TN, {ty T} -> howe D M N T @ -> ofsub G SS D ->
   ofsub G TT D -> howesub G SS TT D -> {SS |- cp M SM} -> {TT |- cp N TN} ->
   howe G SM TN T

howe_substitutive < intros.

       ofsub G SS D -> ofsub G TT D -> howesub G SS TT D ->
       {SS |- cp M SM} -> {TT |- cp N TN} -> howe G SM TN T

H3 : ofsub G SS D
H4 : ofsub G TT D
H5 : howesub G SS TT D
H6 : {SS |- cp M SM}
H7 : {TT |- cp N TN}
============================
 howe G SM TN T
